
add_namespace = fate_of_?

country_event = {
	id = fate_of_?
.1
	title = fate_of_?
.1.t
	desc = fate_of_?
.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = fate_of_?
.1.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					original_tag = ?

					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = ?
	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = ?

					clear_autonomous_states_variable = yes
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	?
_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = ?
_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = PREV	}
				}
			}
			else = {
				?
 = {
					clear_autonomous_states_variable = yes
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	?
_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						?
 = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = ?
_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = ?
	}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_?
.1.1
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				original_tag = ?

				is_subject_of = ROOT
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = ?

					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
						check_variable = {	?
_state_variable = 1	}
					}
					PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
	
add_namespace = fate_of_AFG
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_AFG.1
	title = fate_of_AFG.1.t
	desc = fate_of_AFG.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = fate_of_AFG.1.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					original_tag = AFG
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = AFG	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = AFG
					clear_autonomous_states_variable = yes
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	AFG_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = AFG_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = PREV	}
				}
			}
			else = {
				AFG = {
					clear_autonomous_states_variable = yes
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	AFG_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						AFG = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = AFG_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = AFG	}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_AFG.1.1
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				original_tag = AFG
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = AFG
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
						check_variable = {	AFG_state_variable = 1	}
					}
					PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
	
add_namespace = fate_of_ARM
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_ARM.1
	title = fate_of_ARM.1.t
	desc = fate_of_ARM.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = fate_of_ARM.1.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					original_tag = ARM
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = ARM	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = ARM
					clear_autonomous_states_variable = yes
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	ARM_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = ARM_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = PREV	}
				}
			}
			else = {
				ARM = {
					clear_autonomous_states_variable = yes
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	ARM_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						ARM = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = ARM_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = ARM	}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				original_tag = ARM
				is_subject_of = ROOT

			}
		}

			every_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = ARM
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
						check_variable = {	ARM_state_variable = 1	}
					}
					PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	desc = fate_of_PAL.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = fate_of_PAL.1.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					original_tag = PAL
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = PAL	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = PAL
					clear_autonomous_states_variable = yes
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	PAL_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = PAL_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = PREV	}
				}
			}
			else = {
				PAL = {
					clear_autonomous_states_variable = yes
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	PAL_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						PAL = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = PAL_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = PAL	}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_PAL.1.1
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				original_tag = PAL
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = PAL
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
						check_variable = {	PAL_state_variable = 1	}
					}
					PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					}

add_namespace = fate_of_CAT
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_CAT.1
	title = fate_of_CAT.1.t
	desc = fate_of_CAT.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = fate_of_CAT.1.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					original_tag = CAT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = CAT	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = CAT
					clear_autonomous_states_variable = yes
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	CAT_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CAT_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = PREV	}
				}
			}
			else = {
				CAT = {
					clear_autonomous_states_variable = yes
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	CAT_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						CAT = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CAT_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = CAT	}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_CAT.1.1
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		trigger = {

add_namespace = fate_of_ABK
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_ABK.1
	title = fate_of_ABK.1.t
	desc = fate_of_ABK.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = fate_of_ABK.1.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					original_tag = ABK
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = ABK	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = ABK
					clear_autonomous_states_variable = yes
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	ABK_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = ABK_kingdom

			every_country = {
				limit = {
					original_tag = NMX
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
						check_variable = {	NMX_state_variable = 1	}
					}
					PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
	
add_namespace = fate_of_TEX
country_event = {
	id = fate_of_TEX.1
	title = fate_of_TEX.1.t
	desc = fate_of_TEX.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name = fate_of_TEX.1.0
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				any_country = {
					original_tag = TEX
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {	country_exists = TEX	}
				create_dynamic_country = {
					original_tag = TEX
					clear_autonomous_states_variable = yes
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	TEX_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = TEX_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = PREV	}
				}
			}
			else = {
				TEX = {
					clear_autonomous_states_variable = yes
					every_state = {
						limit = {
							is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
							check_variable = {	TEX_state_variable = 1	}
						}
						TEX = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = TEX_kingdom
					ROOT = {	puppet = TEX	}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = fate_of_TEX.1.1
		ai_chance = {	base = 10	}
		trigger = {
			any_country = {
				original_tag = TEX
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
			}
		}

				limit = {
					original_tag = TEX

						is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
						check_variable = {	TEX_state_variable = 1	}
					}
					PREV = {	transfer_state = PREV	}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
